   **需要注意的是，由于现在分词的主动形式具有形容词的性质，因此它可以在句子中作为定语或者表语。在这个例句中，非限制性定语从句中的“offering”修饰“lands”，相当于“which/that are offering”，表示“正在提供”不同的体验。**

   make是一个非常常见的动词，有很多用法和短语。下面列举一些常见的用法和例子：

   1. **make friends with sb：和某人交朋友。例如：She quickly made friends with her new classmates.**
   2. **make a decision：做决定。例如：It's time for us to make a decision on this matter.**
   3. **make a difference：产生影响。例如：Every little bit helps and can make a difference.**
   4. **make a plan：制定计划。例如：Let's make a plan for our next vacation.**
   5. **make a mistake：犯错误。例如：I made a mistake on the math problem.**
   6. **make an effort：努力尝试。例如：He made an effort to learn a new skill.**
   7. **make progress：取得进展。例如：The company has made great progress in developing new products.**
   8. **make money：赚钱。例如：She started her own business to make money.**
   9. **make sense：有意义、合理。例如：What she said didn't make any sense to me.**
   10. **make sure：确保。例如：Can you make sure that the door is locked before we leave?**

   这些都是make的常见用法和短语，当然还有很多其他的用法和短语。

   1. **make up：组成；化妆；弥补**
      1. **The committee is made up of ten members.（委员会由十名成员组成。）**
      2. **She made up her face before going to the party.（她去聚会前化了妆。）**
      3. **He will have to work overtime to make up the lost time.（他将不得不加班赶时间。）**
   2. **make out：辨认出；理解；填写（表格等）**
      1. **I can't make out what you are saying.（我听不清你在说什么。）**
      2. **It was difficult to make out the meaning of the ancient text.（很难辨认出古代文本的含义。）**
      3. **Could you help me make out this form?（你能帮我填写这张表格吗？）**
   3. **make for：前往；促成**
      1. **They made for the nearest exit.（他们朝最近的出口走去。）**
      2. **This policy will make for greater economic stability.（这项政策将促进更大的经济稳定。）**
   4. **make into：制成；变成**
      1. **She made the clay into a vase.（她把黏土制成了一个花瓶。）**
      2. **He hopes to make his hobby into a career.（他希望把自己的兴趣变成一份职业。）**
   5. **make of：理解；认为**
      1. **I don't know what to make of this situation.（我不知道该如何理解这种情况。）**
      2. **What do you make of his proposal?（你认为他的提议怎么样？）**
   6. **make over：改造；移交**
      1. **The old building was made over into a modern office.（那栋老建筑被改造成了现代化的办公室。）**
      2. **She made over the ownership of the company to her son.（她把公司的所有权移交给了她的儿子。）**
   7. **make through：完成；度过**
      1. **We finally made through the project after many sleepless nights.（我们经过多个不眠之夜，终于完成了这个项目。）**
      2. **I don't know how we're going to make through this difficult time.（我不知道我们该如何度过这个艰难的时期。）**
   8. **make up for：弥补；补偿**
      1. **He tried to make up for his mistake by working harder.（他试图通过更努力地工作来弥补自己的错误。）**
      2. **She brought a gift to make up for missing the party.（她带了一份礼物以弥补缺席聚会的过失。）**

6. <u><font color=red><strong>      In case I forget     </strong></font></u>， please remind me of my bike which is still under repair. (case)

   **万一我忘记**，请提醒我我的自行车还在修理中。

   <font color=red><strong>In case I forget</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>in case“以防万一”,引导条件状语从句。</strong></font>

   - **in my case ：就我来说**

     **In my case I chose that course which I considered right （至于我呢，就选择了我认为正确的那条路线。）**

   - **in my opinion ：我的意见是**

     **In my opinion, I think it is a wonderful country. （我的意见是，这是一个美妙的国度。）**
     
   - **in which case 在那种情况下;那样的话;在那种情况下**

7. Shirley<u><font color=red><strong>     was writing           </strong></font></u>a book about China last year, but I don't know whether she has finished it. (write)

   雪莉去年**在写**一本关于中国的书，但是我不知道她是否已经完成了。

   <font color=red><strong>was writing</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示过去某段时间一直在做的事情用过去进行时。</strong></font>

8. Sydney is the biggest city in Australia, which has many places of interest,<u><font color=red><strong>      among which is      </strong></font></u>the Opera House. (which)

   悉尼是澳大利亚最大的城市,那里有很多名胜古迹,**其中就有**歌剧院。

   <font color=red><strong>among which is</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>此处为“介词+关系代词”引导定语从句,由“其中”可知,介词用among.</strong></font>

   - **places of interest ：名胜古迹**

   - **interest** 

     **n.兴趣;关注;引人关注的性质;吸引力;趣味;业余爱好;利益;利息;好处;（企业或公司的）股份;利害关系;同行**
     **vt.使感兴趣;使关注**

   - **介词+关系代词通常用来引导定语从句，这种结构通常出现在主句的名词或代词后面，用来修饰或说明这个名词或代词。**

     1. **in which: 在其中**
        **例句：This is the museum in which the ancient artifacts are displayed.(这是展示古代文物的博物馆。)**
     2. **of which: 其中的**
        **例句：The house, of which the roof was damaged, needed repairs.(这所屋顶受损的房子需要修理。)**
     3. **for which: 为了哪个**
        **例句：He has bought a new camera for which he paid a lot of money.(他花了很多钱买了一台新相机。)**
     4. **on which: 在哪个上面**
        **例句：The painting, on which he spent many hours, was finally finished.(他花了好几个小时画的这幅画终于完成了。)**
     5. **by which: 通过哪个**
        **例句：This is the method by which we can solve the problem.(这就是我们解决这个问题的方法。)**
     6. **with which: 用哪个**
        **例句：She wrote the letter with the pen with which I had just signed the contract.(她用我刚刚签署合同的钢笔写了这封信。)**
     7. **at which: 在哪个地方**
        **例句：The party will be held at the restaurant at which we had dinner last time.(聚会将在我们上次吃晚饭的餐厅举行。)**
     8. **to which: 到哪个**
        **例句：This is the address to which the letter should be sent.(这是信件应该寄到的地址。)**

   - **在正式的英语书面语中，应该用“for whom”引导定语从句，而不是“for who”。因为“whom”是关系代词，代表宾格，而在定语从句中，关系代词所在的位置相当于一个宾语，应该使用宾格形式。虽然在口语或非正式场合中，人们有时可能会使用“for who”，但这在正式的英语书面语中是不被认可的。**

     **举个例子：**

     - **The scholarship is intended for students for whom English is not their first language.（正确）**

       **该奖学金是为英语不是第一语言的学生准备的**

     - **The scholarship is intended for students for who English is not their first language.（不正确）**

9. He<u><font color=red><strong>       must have completed          </strong></font></u>his work; otherwise he wouldn't be enjoying himself by the seaside.(complete)

   他**肯定完成了**工作,否则他不会在海边玩得这么痛快。

   <font color=red><strong>must have completed</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去情况的肯定推测用 must have done的形式。</strong></font>

   - **"by" 在 "by the seaside" 中作为介词使用。它表示位置，意思是“在……旁边，在……附近”。 "By the seaside" 的意思是“在海边”。**

   - **"Be enjoying oneself"是一个表示正在愉悦地度过时间的短语，通常用来描述某个人在某个活动或场合中感到非常愉快和放松**

     **She is really enjoying herself at the party, chatting with friends and dancing to the music.（她在聚会上玩得很开心，和朋友聊天，跟着音乐跳舞。）**

     **这个短语中的"oneself"是反身代词，表示主语是自己。所以，这个短语通常用于第三人称单数和复数形式。**

10. Two tennis courts as well as a swimming pool<u><font color=red><strong>     are available for        </strong></font></u>the regular members of the club.(available)

    有两个网球场和一个游泳池**供**俱乐部的固定会员**使用**。
    
    <font color=red><strong>are available for</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>as well as连接两个名词时,谓语动词的形式由主语决定,故此处用复数形式; be available for“供……使用,为……所用”。</strong></font>
    
    - **regular :**
    
      **adj.定时的，定期的;固定的;正常的;均匀的;有规律的，**
      **n.常客，正式成员，固定成员，正式职工;**
      **adv.按时地，定期地;经常;完全;非常**
    
    - **regularly**
    
      **adv.有规律地;经常;间隙均匀地;均匀地;匀称地**





## lesson 44

1. The heavy storm<u><font color=red><strong>      dying down    </strong></font></u>at last, everyone on the island felt released.(die)

   狂风暴雨最后**渐渐平息**了,岛上的每个人都松了一口气。

   <font color=red><strong>dying down</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>die down“渐渐平息,渐渐消失”;前后两分句的主语不一致,且没有连接词连接,故用独立主格结构;the heavy storm与 die down之间为逻辑上的主动关系,故用动词-ing形式。</strong></font>

   1. **"At last" 表示最终、终于，强调经历了漫长的等待或困难后终于实现了某事。**

      **We waited for hours for the rain to stop, and at last it cleared up(我们等了好几个小时雨才停下来，最后雨放晴了)**

   2. **Finally：表示最后，终于的意思，常用于描述一件经历漫长等待之后的结果。**

      **Finally, the long-awaited book has been published.**

   3. **Eventually：意为“最终”，“终于”，表示经过一段时间或经历后最终发生的事情。**

      **Eventually, I found the key that I had lost.**

   4. **In the end：意为“最后”，“终究”，表示经历一番波折或经过一段时间的思考后得出的结论或结果。**

      **In the end, I decided to quit my job and pursue my dream.**

   5. **At length：意为“终于”，“最终”，表示经过一段时间或一番波折后最终得到的结果或结论。**

      **At length, the company announced its decision to merge with another firm.**

   6. **Ultimately：意为“最终”，“终究”，表示在经历了一些变化或困难后最终取得的成果或结果。**

      **Ultimately, the team won the championship after a long and hard-fought season.**

   7. **released  作为动词的过去分词，通常表示释放、发行、发布等意思；而作为形容词时，通常表示被释放的、解脱的、放松的等意思。**

   8. **released v.释放;放出;放走;放开;松开;使自由移动(或飞翔、降落等);发泄;**

2. My demand is that the information referred to in my report<u><font color=red><strong>     (should) be sent to          </strong></font></u>Mr Brown without any delay. (send)

   我的要求是,我的报告中提及的信息**要**及时**传送给**布朗先生。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) be sent to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>demand“要求”,之后的表语从句中用虚拟语气,即从句的谓语动词用“should+动词原形”,should可省略;send.. . to sb.“把……传送给某人”,此处send与the information 之间为动宾关系,故用被动语态；"referred to in my report"是过去分词作定语，用于修饰 "the information"，表达被动的意思，即“在我报告中提到的信息”。</strong></font>

   1. **command：命令，要求，控制**
   2. **mandate：授权，命令，要求**
   3. **request：请求，要求**
   4. **require：要求，需要**
   5. **claim：索要，要求**
   6. **solicit：请求，恳求**
   7. **entreat：请求，乞求**

   这些单词都有表示“要求，请求，控制”等意义，但在不同的语境中可能会有细微的区别。

3. Our school, which<u><font color=red><strong>    was set up         </strong></font></u>in 1945，lies in the south of Changchun City. (set)

   我们学校**建于**1945年,位于长春市的南部。

   <font color=red><strong>was set up</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>set up“建立”,与our school之间为动宾关系,故用被动语态,且由时间状语in 1945可知用一般过去时。</strong></font>

   1. **Set up: 建立、设立 例如: We need to set up a meeting to discuss the new project. (我们需要设立一次会议来讨论新项目。)**
   2. **Set off: 出发、启程 例如: We set off early in the morning to avoid traffic. (我们一早出发以避开交通拥堵。)**
   3. **Settle down: 安定下来、定居 例如: After years of traveling, she finally settled down in a small town. (多年的旅行之后，她最终在一个小镇安定下来。)**
   4. **Set aside: 留出、拨出 例如: He always sets aside time for exercise every day. (他每天都会留出时间进行锻炼。)**
   5. **Set out: 开始、出发、列举 例如: She set out to write a novel last year. (去年她开始写小说。) / The report sets out the details of the investigation. (这份报告列举了调查的详细内容。)**
   6. **Set back: 推迟、延误 例如: The bad weather has set back our construction schedule. (恶劣的天气延误了我们的建设进度。)**
   7. **Set in: 开始、到来 例如: The cold weather has set in early this year. (今年寒冷天气来得早。)**
   8. **Settle up: 结清、付清账款 例如: I need to settle up with the landlord before moving out. (我需要在搬出前结清与房东的账款。)**

4. The more careful you are in the exam,<u><font color=red><strong>       the fewer mistakes        </strong></font></u>you will make. (mistake)

   考试中你越细心，你犯的**错误就越少**。

   <font color=red><strong>the fewer mistakes</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由前半句中的the more和“越”可知,该句用了“the+比较级...,the+比较级...”结构;mistake为可数名词,故用 few修饰具复效形式，具比较级为fewer。</strong></font>

5. The man has been out of work for almost four years. He<u><font color=red><strong>     must have experienced      </strong></font></u>a lot of difficulties. (experience)

   这个人已经失业将近四年了。他**一定经历了**很多困难。

   <font color=red><strong>must have experienced</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去清况的肯定的推测用must have done的形式。</strong></font>

   - **difficulty : n.困难;难题;难事;**

   - **difficult ：adj.困难的;费力的;**

   - **different ：adj.不同的;有区别的;有差异的;分别的;**

     It's different now than it was a year ago.

   - **differently ：adv.不同地；相异地**

     Every individual learns differently...（每个人的学习方式都不一样。）

   - **difference ：n.差别;差异;不同(之处);**

     What's the difference between high school and college?（高中和大学之间有什么不同？）

6. Danny left word with my secretary<u><font color=red><strong>     that he would leave       </strong></font></u>in the afternoon. (leave)

   丹尼给我的秘书留言说下午**他就离开**。

   <font color=red><strong>that he would leave</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>that 引导同位语从句,用来解释说明word的内容,that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略; leave表示的动作是从过去某个时间看来将要发生的,故用过去将来时。</strong></font>

   **leave sth with sb : 把某物交给某人**

7. The play may be several hours late, in which case<u><font color=red><strong>     there is no point（in） waiting      </strong></font></u>.(point)

   这部戏可能要晚几个小时，那样的话**等着就没有意义了**。

   <font color=red><strong>there is no point（in） waiting</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>There is/was no point in doing sth.“做某事没有意义”,其中in可省略。</strong></font>

   **in which case 在那种情况下;那样的话;在那种情况下**

8. Do you know <u><font color=red><strong>     where I can find    </strong></font></u> a second-hand carpet cleaner? （find)

   你知道**我在哪里可以找到**一个二手的地毯吸尘器吗?

   <font color=red><strong>where I can find</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>where引导宾语从句,开在从句中作地点状语,宾语从句中用陈述语序。</strong></font>

9. Mother always tells me that<u><font color=red><strong>     helping others      </strong></font></u>is the source of happiness. (help)

   妈妈总是告诉我,**帮助别人**是快乐的源泉。

   <font color=red><strong>helping others</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导的宾语从句中缺少主语,应用动词-ing形式的短语作从句主语,表示某种概念或经验。</strong></font>

   - **happiness : n.幸福;愉快;(用语等的)适当;幸运**
   - **kindness ：n.仁慈;善良;体贴;宽容;友好的举动**
   - **source ：n.来源;出处;信息来源;原始资料;**
   - **resource ：n.资源;财力;有助于实现目标的东西;资料;勇气;才智;谋略**
     **vt.向…提供资金(或设备)**

10. The teacher and the students<u><font color=red><strong>    were visiting       </strong></font></u>the museum when the earthquake struck. (visit)

    地震发生时，老师和学生们**正在参观**博物馆。

    <font color=red><strong>were visiting</strong></font>

    <strong>解析：</strong>

    <font color=red><strong>表示过去某个时间正在进行的动作用过去进行时,且主语为 the teacher and the students,故谓语动词用复数形式。</strong></font>
    
    **【不规则形式】 strike struck, struck**





## lesson 45

1. The commander gave the order that all the soldiers<u><font color=red><strong>      should stay where they were        </strong></font></u>that night. (stay)

   指挥官下命令说，所有的士兵当晚都**应该待在他们所在的地方**。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) stay where they were</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>order“命令”,其后的同位语从句中用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should+动词原形”,should可省略;stay后的宾语从句中引导词在句中作地点状语,故用 where。</strong></font>

2. Do you know the singer and dancer who<u><font color=red><strong>    is standing at the gate       </strong></font></u>?(stand)

   你认识**正站在门口**的那个歌唱家兼舞蹈家吗?

   <font color=red><strong>is standing at the gate</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>the singer and dancer指兼有歌唱家和舞蹈家两个身份的同一个人,故谓语动词用单数形式;表示“在门口”应用介词at;由句意可知用现在进行时。</strong></font>

3. I know I was a naive fool to trust him, but he is a real charmer who totally<u><font color=red><strong>        took me in          </strong></font></u>.(take)

   我知道我是个天真的傻瓜，竟然相信他但是他真的是一个善于施展魅力的人，**让我**完全**受骗了**。

   <font color=red><strong>took me in</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由“I was a naive fool to trust him”可知,“他欺骗我”是发生在过去的事情,故用一般过去时; take in“欺骗”。</strong></font>

   **totally : adv.完全地;完全;全部地;整个地**

4. Not<u><font color=red><strong>      knowing her address           </strong></font></u>，I might as well telephone her to come over. (know)

   我不**知道她的地址**，我还不如打电话让她过来。

   <font color=red><strong>knowing her address</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>现在分词短语"Not knowing her address"，它作为原因状语，表明我不知道她的地址是为什么我需要打电话给她；将分词短语"Not knowing her address"改写成普通句子时，需要加上主语和谓语动词，同时将分词短语转化为一个从句，可以改写为："Because I don't know her address, I might as well telephone her to come over." 或者 "As I don't know her address, I might as well telephone her to come over." 这两个句子的意思是一样的，只是表达方式略有不同。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>I 与not know之间为逻辑上的主动关系,故用动词-ing形式作状语,表示原因。</strong></font>

   - **might as well  只好(做);(做…)也无妨;(几乎)和…一样**

     If no one else wants it, we might as well give it to him. （如果没人要这个，我们不妨给他吧。）

   -  **come over  过来;抓住;发生;**

   - **"As well"是一个常用的短语，在英语中有多种用法：**

     1. **"As well" 可以表示“也、同样”。例如：“She speaks Spanish as well as French.”（她不仅会说法语，也会说西班牙语。）**
     2. **"As well" 也可以表示“也要、也可以”。例如：“I'll have a coffee as well.”（我也要一杯咖啡。）**
     3. **"As well" 还可以表示“此外、另外、还有”。例如：“We need eggs, milk, and bread. Oh, and butter as well.”（我们需要鸡蛋、牛奶和面包。哦，还有黄油。）**
     4. **"As well" 还可以表示“同样地、也一样”。例如：“He's always working hard and expects others to do the same as well.”（他总是很努力工作，也期待别人也一样。）**

5. They sometimes<u><font color=red><strong>      found it is difficult/hard to concentrate        </strong></font></u>when reading, but fortunately, their teacher helped them out at last. (concentrate)

   有时候他们**发现**阅读时**集中注意力很困难**，但幸运的是，他们的老师最终帮助他们解决了问题。

   <font color=red><strong>found it is difficult/hard to concentrate</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式宾语，真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

   **help sb out ：帮助某人;帮助某人解决难题，帮助某人摆脱困境，帮助某人完成工作**

6. It was still uncertain<u><font color=red><strong>        whether he would go along           </strong></font></u>with us to visit our teacher. (go)

   还不确定**他是否会**和我们**一起去**探望我们的老师。

   <font color=red><strong>whether he would go along</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的从句,whether引导主语从句,意为“是否”"；因为主句中使用的是过去时态的"was"，所以从句中要使用相应的过去时态来保持时态的一致，即"whether he would go"。</strong></font>

   <strong>"go along with"是一个英语短语，表示同意或支持某人或某事物，也可以表示跟随或一起前往某处。可以用中文翻译为“支持，赞同”或“跟随，一起前往”。例如：</strong>

   - <strong>I will go along with your plan.（我会支持你的计划。）</strong>
   - <strong>She decided to go along with her friends to the party.（她决定和她的朋友一起去参加聚会。）</strong>

7. It is the protection of trees<u><font color=red><strong>      that matters         </strong></font></u>,rather than how many trees are planted. (matter)

   **重要的**是保护树木而非种了多少树木。

   <font color=red><strong>that matters</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>该句中用到了强调句式“It+be+被强调部分+that...”,被强调部分为“the protection of trees”,其中 that不能省略。</strong></font>

8. Their performance includes rhythm and rhyming words as well as tongue twister, which<u><font color=red><strong>    makes the audience applaud       </strong></font></u>.(make)

   他们的表演包括节奏、韵律以及绕口令,这些使他们经常**赢得观众的掌声**。

   <font color=red><strong>makes the audience applaud</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>make后跟不带to的不定式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

9. One should stick to<u><font color=red><strong>   whatever he has begun/started    </strong></font></u>no matter how difficult it is. (whatever)

   一个人应该坚持**他已经开始的任何事情**,不管有多么困难。

   <font color=red><strong>whatever he has begun/started</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>whatever引导宾语从句,开在从句中作宾语。</strong></font>

   **"Stick to"是一个短语动词，意为“坚持；遵守；忠于”。例如：**

   - **You should stick to your goals if you want to succeed.（如果你想成功，你应该坚持自己的目标。）**
   - **He always sticks to his principles, no matter what.（无论发生什么，他总是遵守自己的原则。）**
   - **I'll stick to the plan we agreed on.（我会遵守我们达成的计划。）**

   **常见的搭配有：**

   - **stick to + 名词：坚持做某事、遵守规定、保持信念等；**
   - **stick to + 动词原形：坚持某种习惯或做法、坚持自己的决定等；**
   - **stick to + 代词/名词/动词-ing：坚持某个方向、坚持自己的观点、坚持自己的工作等。**

10. No sooner had I entered the classroom<u><font color=red><strong>       than the bell rang      </strong></font></u>.(ring)

    我刚一-进入教室,**铃就响了**。
    
    <font color=red><strong>than the bell rang</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>no sooner.. . than.. .“—……就…·引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>





## lesson 46

1. Although that lady is very young, she has two children, who are<u><font color=red><strong>      of the same age      </strong></font></u>.(of)

   尽管那位女士非常年轻,但是她已经有两个孩子了,**他们的年龄一样**。

   <font color=red><strong>of an age/of the same age</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“年龄相同”应用be of an age或be of the same age.</strong></font>

   **She learned to swim at the age of five.**

   **她在五岁时学会了游泳**

2. We regret<u><font color=red><strong>     to inform you       </strong></font></u>that we have no positions available for someone of your excellent qualifications. (inform)

   我们很遗憾地**通知您**，我们没有适合您这种有杰出资历的人的职位。

   <font color=red><strong>to inform you</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>regret后跟不定式表示对将要做的事情感到遗憾。</strong></font>

   - **position**

     **n.位置;地方;恰当位置;正确位置;vt.安装;安置;使处于**

   - **excellent** 

     **adj.杰出的;极好的;非凡的;**

   - **qualification**

     **n.(通过经验或具备技能而取得的)资格;资历;学历;限定条件;获得资格**

3. I'm afraid you cannot listen to the weather report now. The radio I<u><font color=red><strong>       had repaired         </strong></font></u>yesterday is broken again today. (repair)

   恐怕你现在不能听天气预报。昨天我**让人修**的收音机今天又坏了。

   <font color=red><strong>had repaired</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>have后可跟动词-ed形式作宾语补足语,表示the radio是repair这一列作的承受者;结合时间状语yesterday可知用一般过去时；have sth. done“使某物被做”</strong></font>

4. The young coach must have thought Johnson was worth it, or she<u><font color=red><strong>      wouldn't have wasted        </strong></font></u>so much time on him. (waste)

   年轻的教练一定认为约翰逊值得这样，否则她**不会**在他身上**浪费**那么多时间。

   <font color=red><strong>couldn't/wouldn't nave wasted</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由语境及关键词or可知,此处是对过去情沉的否定虚拟,此时主句谓语动词用couldn't/wouldn't have done的形式。</strong></font>

   be worth to：值得做

5. <u><font color=red><strong>   It is a matter of time         </strong></font></u>before they will discover that John has left. (matter)

   他们会发现约翰已经离开了,**这只是个时间问题**。

   <font color=red><strong>It is a matter of time</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的从句。</strong></font>

6. Guess <u><font color=red><strong>    whom I came across           </strong></font></u>in the town yesterday! My primary school maths teacher! (come)

   猜猜我昨天在镇上**碰到了谁**!我的小学数学老师!

   <font color=red><strong>who/whom I came across</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>who/whom引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语,不能省略;come across“偶遇,碰到”。</strong></font>

   **Guess：**

   - **vt. 猜测；认为；推测；猜中**
   - **vi. 猜；推测；猜中**
   - **n. 猜测；推测**

7. He lost his job and meanwhile, the house was too expensive, so he couldn't afford<u><font color=red><strong>       to buy it         </strong></font></u>.(buy)

   他失业了，同时房子也太贵了,因此他**买不起**。

   <font color=red><strong>to buy it</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>afford后跟不定式作宾语。</strong></font>

   **meanwhile**

   - **adv. 与此同时；在此期间；另一方面**
   - **n. 其间，其时**

   **afford to do :有经济条件做某事，负担得起做**

8. Sometimes cells either divide too fast or at the wrong time,<u><font color=red><strong>        which makes it difficult        </strong></font></u>for the body to function properly. (make)

   有时细胞要么分裂得太快要么分裂得不是时候,**这使**身体难以准确地运行。

   <font color=red><strong>which makes it difficult</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>which引导非限制性定语从句,引导词指前面整个分句提到的事实,并在从句中作主语,故谓语动词用单数形式;it在从句中作形式宾语,真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

   1. **properly：*adv.*正确地，适当地；得体地，恰当地；实际上，严格地说；彻底地**

   2. **function ：**

      - **n. 功能，职责；宴会，典礼；函数，应变量；由其他事情造成的结果；子例行程序，子例程；官能团，功能团**
      - **v. 工作，运转；行使职责，发挥功能**

   3. **"Either", "neither", 和 "nor" 都是用于表示否定选择或否定关系的词语，它们在句子中起到连接的作用。**

      1. **"Either" （或者）用于表示在两个选择之间的肯定关系。它通常与 "or" 连用，用于在肯定的选择之间做出选择。**

         **例如：**

         1. **You can either have tea or coffee. （你可以喝茶或咖啡。）**
         2. **Either John or Mary will pick you up from the airport. （要么是约翰，要么是玛丽会去机场接你。）**

      2. **"Neither" （也不）用于表示否定的选择关系。它通常与 "nor" 连用，用于否定的选择之间。**

         **例如：**

         1. **Neither Tom nor Sarah could attend the meeting. （汤姆和莎拉都不能参加会议。）**
         2. **I have neither the time nor the resources to complete the project. （我既没有时间也没有资源完成这个项目。）**

      3. **"Nor" （也不）用于否定句中，连接两个否定要素。它常与 "neither" 连用，形成否定选择关系。**

         **例如：**

         1. **I don't like coffee, nor do I like tea. （我不喜欢咖啡，也不喜欢茶。）**
         2. **He didn't study for the test, nor did he ask for help. （他没有为考试学习，也没有寻求帮助。）**

      **总结起来，"either" 表示肯定选择关系，"neither" 表示否定选择关系，而 "nor" 用于否定句中连接两个否定要素。**

9. The news<u><font color=red><strong>          that the plane would take off        </strong></font></u>on time made everyone at the airport happy. (take)

   **飞机将**按时**起飞**的消息让机场里的每个人都很高兴。

   <font color=red><strong>that the plane would take off</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导同位语从句,用来解释说明news的内容, that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略;take off“起飞”。</strong></font>

10. The film<u><font color=red><strong>      might have ended        </strong></font></u>by now, because the crowd are flooding out of the cinema (end)

    现在电影**大概已经结束了**，因为人群正从电影院里涌出来。
    
    <font color=red><strong>may/might have ended</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>表示“大概”应用情态动词may或might;此处表示对过去情况的推测,其后接have done的形式。</strong></font>
    





## lesson 47

1. She<u><font color=red><strong>        must have had          </strong></font></u>a very hard time, for her good friend couldn't recognize her when they met in a park years later. (have)

   她**一定度过了**一段非常艰难的时光，因为多年以后她的好朋友和她在公园里相遇时认不出她了。

   <font color=red><strong>must have had</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去情况的肯定推测用 must have done的形式。</strong></font>

2. As a nurse,<u><font color=red><strong>      what she wants to do       </strong></font></u>is to look after the orphans coming from that poor mountain area.(what)

   作为护士，**她想要做的**就是照顾那些来自那个贫穷山区的孤儿们。

   <font color=red><strong>what she wants to do</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>what引导主语从,并在从句中作宾语；现在分词短语coming from作定语</strong></font>

   **orphan**

   - **n. 孤儿**
   - **v. 成为孤儿**

3. Rich countries have a responsibility towards poor countries and must do<u><font color=red><strong>       all what they can          </strong></font></u>to help others. (can)

   富裕的国家对贫穷的国家有责任,并且必须尽**他们所能**去帮助他人。

   <font color=red><strong>all(that)/what they can</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>what 引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语,相当于 all that,其中 that 可省略。</strong></font>

   - **have a responsibility towards ：对…有责任**
   - **be responsible for :对……负责；是……的原因**

4. As time went by, the new idiom <u><font color=red><strong>     came into being      </strong></font></u>and was widely used later. (come)

   随着时间的流逝，这个新习语**产生了,**并且接着就被广泛使用。

   <font color=red><strong>came into being</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>come into being“产生出现”,由句中时态可知用般过去时。</strong></font>

   - **as time go by：随着时间的推移**

     **As time go by my memory seem to get worse.** 

     **随著时间的流逝，我的记忆力似乎越来越差。**

   - **idiom**

     **n. 习语，成语；方言，土话；（个人、艺术形式等的）风格，特色**

   - **idiot**

     **n. 白痴，笨蛋；<古>弱智者，低能儿**

5. Whenever he was asked why he was late for class, he would answer carelessly, always<u><font color=red><strong>    saying the same excuse         </strong></font></u>.(say)

   不管什么时候问他为什么上课迟到,他都心不在焉地回答，总是**说同样的借口**。

   <font color=red><strong>saying the same excuse</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>he 与 say 之间为逻辑上的主动关系，故用动词-ing形式作伴随状语。</strong></font>

6. <u><font color=red><strong>        How do you respond to        </strong></font></u>someone who proposes constructing the world's tallest building? (respond)

   **你如何回应**建议建造世界最高建筑的人?

   <font color=red><strong>How do you respond to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>此为 how 引导的特殊疑问句；respond后跟宾语时，宾语前应加介词 to。</strong></font>

   1. **propose ：提议做某事**

      **What do you propose doing next?**

   2. **purpose**

      ***n.*目的，意图；目标，计划；（达到生活中目标的）决心**

      ***v.*有意，打算**

   3. **construct**

      ***v.*建造，修建；组成，创立，构思；绘制，作图**

      ***n.*构想，观念；**

7. When the poor man came to life, he found himself<u><font color=red><strong>     tied to a tree        </strong></font></u>.(tie)

   当这个穷人醒过来的时候,他发现自己**被绑在一棵树上**。

   <font color=red><strong>tied to a tree</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>find 后可跟动词-ed 形式作宾语补足语，表被动和完成，表示himself是tie 这一动作的承受者;tie...to...“把··...·绑在.....上”。</strong></font>

8. He <u><font color=red><strong>       who has passed      </strong></font></u>the exam will be given the driving license. (pass)

   **已经通过**考试的人将会得到驾照。

   <font color=red><strong>who has passed</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>who引导定语从句,并在从句中作主语,由句意及句子结构可知用现在完成时。</strong></font>

9. How I wish I<u><font color=red><strong>        hadn't tried        </strong></font></u>to repair the watch! I only made it worse. (try)

   我多么希望自己**没有尽力**去修这块表!我只是把它搞得更糟了。

   <font color=red><strong>hadn't tried</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>wish 后跟宾语从句时,从句用虚拟语气，且此处表示与过去事实相反,故谓语动词用过去完成时。</strong></font>

10. When driving on the mountain area, we saw signs everywhere warning people<u><font color=red><strong>     to look out for        </strong></font></u>falling rocks. (look)

    当在山区驾驶的时候，我们看到到处都是提醒人们**当心**落石的警示语。
    
    <font color=red><strong>to look out for</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>warn 后跟不定式作宾语补足语;look out for“当心,小心”</strong></font>
    
    1. **warn sb not to do**
    
       **警告不要做**
    
    2. **warn sb to do**
    
       **提醒某人去做某事**





##  lesson 48

1. About 10% of the people on the earth now<u><font color=red><strong>      don't have access to       </strong></font></u>clean drinking water. (access)

   地球上大约10%的人现在**不能喝到**干净的饮用水。

   <font color=red><strong>don't have access to/have no access to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>“百分数+名词”作主语时,谓语动词的单复数由该名词决定,故此处用复数形式; </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>have access to“可接近,可以达到,可以使用”,此处用否定形式,可借助助动词do和可直接用no access.</strong></font>

2. I can't read the advertisement on the board. Could you hold the light<u><font color=red><strong>      closer to it          </strong></font></u>? (close)

   我看不到公告板上的广告。你能把灯拿得**离它近一点**吗?

   <font color=red><strong>closer to it</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>close的副词形式仍为close,其比较级形式为closer; close应与介词to搭配。</strong></font>

   **abroad：国外**

3. <u><font color=red><strong>        The first time I saw            </strong></font></u><u><font color=red><strong>  </strong></font></u>her, I thought she was very gentle and kind-hearted. (time)

   **我第一次**看见她时，我以为她非常温柔善良。

   <font color=red><strong>The first time I saw</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>名词短语the first time可用来引导时间状语从句,表示“第一次……的时候”</strong></font>

   - **gentle ：adj. 文静的，温柔的；v. 使（或变）温柔**

   - **polite：有礼貌的，客气的；礼节性的，客套的；上流的，有教养的；**

   - **courteous：有礼貌的，谦恭的；**

   - **hearted ：**

     **adj. 呈……心情的；有……之心的；放在心上的**

     **v. 铭记；用心材支撑；结心（heart 的过去分词）**

4. I happened<u><font color=red><strong>        to have talked with         </strong></font></u>the man interviewing me before I came here. (talk)

   我在来这里之前刚好**和**面试我的人**说过话**。

   <font color=red><strong>to have talked with </strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>happen后跟不定式作宾语;由“说过话”或者before I came here可知,应用完成时;talk with“与……谈话”。</strong></font>

5. Are you really reading the newspaper? You<u><font color=red><strong>     are holding it upside down         </strong></font></u>,So don't cheat me any more. (hold)

   你真的在读这张报纸吗?你**把它拿倒了**，所以不要再骗我了。

   <font color=red><strong>are holding it upside down</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示现在正在进行的动作用现在进行时;upside down“上下颠倒”。</strong></font>

6. So fast<u><font color=red><strong>       did he run         </strong></font></u>that I couldn't catch up with him though I was already out of breath. (run)

   **他跑得**如此快以至于我追不上他,尽管我已经上气不接下气了

   <font color=red><strong>did he run</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>so...that...结构中的so修饰的副词置于句首时主句应用部分倒装。</strong></font>

7. I suggested that he<u><font color=red><strong>      (should) adapt to             </strong></font></u>the new condition as soon as possible, or it would be difficult for him to carry on.(adapt)

   我建议他尽快**适应**新环境，否则他将很难继续下去。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) adapt to </strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>suggest意为“建议”时,其后的宾语从句中用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should＋动词原形”,should可省略;adapt to“适应”。</strong></font>

   **as soon as possible ：尽快 /尽可能快 /越快越好 /尽可能**

8. <u><font color=red><strong>        why that photo became        </strong></font></u>his greatest glory was a very interesting story. (become)

   **为什么那张照片成了**他最大的荣耀是一个非常有趣的故事。

   <font color=red><strong>Why that photo/picture became</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>why 引导主语从句,并在从句中作原因状语。</strong></font>

9. They keep<u><font color=red><strong>        asking me to join       </strong></font></u>their social club but I prefer to go my own way. (ask)

   他们一直**让我加人**他们的社交俱乐部,但是我更愿意走自己的路。

   <font color=red><strong>asking me to join</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>keep后跟动词-ing形式作宾语;ask后跟不定式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"keep doing"：表示持续进行某种行为，指继续做之前已经在进行的动作。这个结构中，动词以现在分词形式（-ing 形式）出现。</strong></font>

10. The two things in<u><font color=red><strong>       which they take pride         </strong></font></u>are Jim's watch and Lucy's hair.(pride)

    **他们引以为豪**的两件东西是吉姆的表和露西的头发。
    
    <font color=red><strong>which they take pride</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>take pride in“以……为自豪”;该短语中的介词in提至从句句首,且先行词指物,故只能用which引导定语从句。</strong></font>
    
    **be proud of：为..感到骄傲，以...自豪**





##  lesson 49

1. The problem is<u><font color=red><strong>     far from being        </strong></font></u>solved, so it has to be discussed again.(far)

   问题**远没有**解决，因此还得再讨论一次

   <font color=red><strong>far from being</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>far from“远离”;介词from后应跟动词-ing形式。</strong></font>

   **"Far from" 是一个常用的短语，表示距离或程度上的远离，也可用来表示与预期或期望相反。以下是它的几种常见用法：**

   1. **表示距离：指两个地点或物体之间的远离。**
      - **The hotel is far from the airport.（酒店离机场很远。）**
      - **The grocery store is far from our house.（杂货店离我们家很远。）**

   2. **表示程度：表示某事物超出了一定程度，表达程度上的强调。**
      - **He is far from happy about the situation.（他对这种情况远非满意。）**
      - **The performance was far from perfect.（这次表演远非完美。）**

   3. **表示与预期或期望相反：表示某事与人们的预期或期望相反。**
      - **The result was far from what I expected.（结果与我预期的迥然不同。）**
      - **The movie was far from being entertaining.（这部电影远非有趣。）**
   4. **远非做某事：表示某人没有或不愿意做某事。**
      - **He is far from being helpful.（他远非乐于助人。）**
      - **The company is far from meeting its sales targets.（该公司远未达到销售目标。）**
   5. **远非达到某种状态或水平：表示未达到预期的状态或水平。**
      - **The project is far from completion.（这个项目远未完成。）**
      - **Her performance is far from satisfactory.（她的表现远未令人满意。）**
   6. **远非具备某种特征或品质：表示与某种特征或品质相反或迥异。**
      - **The situation is far from ideal.（这种情况远非理想。）**
      - **The product is far from perfect.（这个产品远非完美。）**

   **需要注意的是，"far from" 通常与动词、形容词、副词等修饰词连用，用来描述距离或程度上的远离。**

2. Only by changing the way we live<u><font color=red><strong>     can we save      </strong></font></u>the earth. (save)

   只有通过改变我们的生活方式，**我们才能拯救**地球。

   <font color=red><strong>can we save</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>only强调状语置于句首时句子用部分倒装,根据句意,助动词用can。</strong></font>

3. Water, which seems so simple and common, is<u><font color=red><strong>          what makes life possible        </strong></font></u>.(what)

   水看似如此简单、普通，却是**使生命成为可能的东西。**

   <font color=red><strong>what makes life possible</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>what 引导表语从句,并在从句中作主语;make后可跟形容词作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

4. If<u><font color=red><strong>          I were you          </strong></font></u>,I would never say such kind of words to my younger brother or sister. (be)

   如果**我是你**，我永远不会对我的弟弟或妹妹说这样的话。

   <font color=red><strong>I were you</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>if引导的非真实条件句中,表示与现在事实相反的虚拟语气时,作从句谓语的be动词应用 were.</strong></font>

5. The development of technology has<u><font color=red><strong>       made it possible      </strong></font></u>for us to get in touch with each other more easily. (make)

   科技的发展**使**我们更加容易地联系彼此**成为可能**。

   <font color=red><strong>made it possible</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式宾语,真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

   **get in touch with：和…联系**

   1. **Be connected/related to: 表示两个事物之间存在联系或关联。**

      **This book is connected to the author's personal experiences. （这本书与作者的个人经历有关。）**

   2. **Have a connection/relationship with: 表示具有某种联系或关系。**

      **I have a close relationship with my sister. （我和我的姐姐有着亲密的关系。）**

   3. **Be associated with: 表示某事物与另一事物相关或有关联。**

      **The color red is often associated with love and passion. （红色常常与爱情和激情相关联。）**

   4. **Have ties/links with: 表示具有某种关联或联系。**

      **The company has strong ties with international partners. （该公司与国际合作伙伴有着紧密的联系。）**

   5. **Be in connection/communication with: 表示与某人或某组织进行联系或交流。**

      **I am in communication with the customer support team regarding my issue. （我正在与客户支持团队联系，解决我的问题。）**

6. He may go to the seaside with us today<u><font color=red><strong>      providing that he arrives          </strong></font></u>on time.(provide)

   **如果他**按时**到达**，他可能今天和我们一起去海边。

   <font color=red><strong>providing/provided （that） he arrives </strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>providing/provided that可用来引导条件状语从句,其中that可省略。</strong></font>

   **"providing that"和"provided that"都可以用来引导条件状语从句。它们的意思相同，表示在满足某个条件的情况下才会发生或成立。这两个短语可以互换使用，用法上没有明显的区别。**

   **以下是一个例子：**

   - **You can borrow my car provided that you return it by tomorrow morning.**

     **只要你明天早上之前归还，你可以借我的车。**

   **在这个句子中，"provided that"引导了一个条件状语从句，表明借车的条件是在明天早上之前归还车辆。**

7. She<u><font color=red><strong>        got into a panic        </strong></font></u>when she thought that she'd forgotten the tickets. (panic)

   当想起自己忘记了票时，她**陷入了恐慌**。

   <font color=red><strong>got into a panic</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>get into a panic“陷入恐慌中”。</strong></font>

8. The schools of the future will probably be quite different from<u><font color=red><strong>     what they are      </strong></font></u>today. (what)

   未来的学校很可能和**它们**现在的**样子**很不同。

   <font color=red><strong>what they are</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>what引导宾语从句,并在从句中作表语。</strong></font>

   **probably ：adv. 大概，或许**

   **probable ：adj. 很可能发生（或存在等）的，大概的**

9. Your radio doesn't work. I think you should<u><font color=red><strong>     have it repaired       </strong></font></u>this afternoon, so that you can listen to the music charts tonight. (have)

   你的收音机坏了。我认为今天下午你应该**找人把它修一下**，以便今晚你能听音乐排行榜。

   <font color=red><strong>have it repaired</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>have后可跟动词-ed形式作宾语补足语,表示it是repair这一动作的承受者。</strong></font>

10. Tony is not doing homework in his study. He<u><font color=red><strong>       must be watching         </strong></font></u>TV in the living room now.(must)

    托尼没有在他的书房里写作业。他现在**肯定**在客厅里**看**电视。

    <font color=red><strong>must be watching</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>对正在进行的动作表示肯定推测用must be doing.</strong></font>





# part 08

##  lesson 50

1. My family make it a rule<u><font color=red><strong>     to turn off the TV      </strong></font></u>while having dinner. (turn)

   我家定了一条规则，吃晚饭时**关掉电视**。

   <font color=red><strong>to turn off the TV</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>在此句中,it 作形式宾语,动词不定式短语作真正宾语。</strong></font>

2. <u><font color=red><strong>         That she has been admitted to      </strong></font></u>Wuhan University made her family go wild with joy. (admit)

   **她已经**被武汉大学**录取**，这使得她的家人欣喜若狂。

   <font color=red><strong>That she has been admitted to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>此处主语从句由连词 that引导,that 在句中不作句子成分，主句的时态是一般过去式，从句用现在完成时的被动。</strong></font>

   1. **be admitted to** 

      **加入；获准做某事**

      **be admitted to university**

      **被大学录取**

      **join in、make in**

      **加入；获准做某事**

   2. **admit to**

      **承认；许可进入**

      **accept、agree、recognize、acknowledge、grant**

   3. **admit to doing**

      **承认做了某事承认做过详细翻译**

   4. **go wild with joy ：欣喜若狂**

3. <u><font color=red><strong>       Seen from a distance           </strong></font></u>,the island looked like a cloud, (see)

   **从远处看**,小岛就像一朵云。

   <font color=red><strong>Seen from a distance</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>the island 与 see 之间是被动关系,故用动词-ed 形式作条件状语。</strong></font>

   1. **distance ：**

      **n.远处；疏远，隔阂；（人或物之间的）差别，差距；进展；距离**

      ***v.*疏远，远离**

      **adj.远距离的**

      **distance education ：远程教育**

   2. **distinct from种类不同与种类种类差别**

   3. **in the distance**

      **A plane was droning in the distance.**

      **飞机在远处嗡嗡地响。**

   4. **from a distance**

      **从远处；隔开一段距离**

4. Some of the people<u><font color=red><strong>   invited to the party     </strong></font></u>can't come tonight.(invite)

   有些**受邀参加聚会**的人今晚不能来了。

   <font color=red><strong>invited to the party/who have been invited to the party</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>这里的定语或定语从句都修饰前面的 people一词。</strong></font>

5. <u><font color=red><strong>     However far it is         </strong></font></u>,I intend to drive there today. (far)

   **不管有多远**，我今天打算开车去那里。

   <font color=red><strong>However far it is</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>however 一词引导让步状语从句。</strong></font>

   1. **Intend to do something：打算做某事**
      - **I intend to visit my parents next weekend.**
      - **She intends to start a new business.**
   2. **Plan to do something：计划做某事**
      - **We are planning to go on vacation in the summer.**
      - **They have planned to hold a meeting next month.**
   3. **Be going to do something：打算做某事**
      - **I'm going to study abroad next year.**
      - **He's going to buy a new car.**
   4. **Have plans to do something：有计划做某事**
      - **She has plans to learn a musical instrument.**
      - **They have plans to renovate their house.**
   5. **Be considering doing something：考虑做某事**
      - **We are considering moving to a bigger city.**
      - **He is considering changing his career.**

6. <u><font color=red><strong>        It occurred to me        </strong></font></u> that I left my mobile phone in the taxi. (occur)

   **我突然想起**我把手机落在了出租车里。

   <font color=red><strong>It occurred to me</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>It occurred to sb,that..表示"某人突然想起某事"</strong></font>

7. I received a message<u><font color=red><strong>     that he may/might arrive         </strong></font></u>late. (arrive)

   我收到信息，说**他可能**晚**到**。

   <font color=red><strong>that he may/might arrive</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导同位语从句，说明message的具体内容;由句意“可能·····.”可知情态动词用may 或 might.</strong></font>

8. It was the first time that I<u><font color=red><strong>     had driven         </strong></font></u>a taxi. (drive)

   那是我**第一次**开出租车。

   <font color=red><strong>have driven</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>It was the first time...句型中用过去完成时。</strong></font>

9. The machine<u><font color=red><strong>    was being repaired     </strong></font></u>at this time yesterday. (repair)

   昨天这个时候机器**正在被修理。**

   <font color=red><strong>was being repaired</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由于机器在昨天这个时候正在被修理所以用过去进行时的被动语态形式。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>     The harder you study      </strong></font></u>,the more progress you will make. (hard)

    **你学习越努力**，取得的进步就会越大。

    <font color=red><strong>The harder you study</strong></font>

    <strong>解析：</strong>

    <font color=red><strong>“the+比较级...,the+比较级...表示“越.....·越......”。</strong></font>
    
    **progress ：*n.*进步，进展；前进，行进；（社会的）进步；*v.*进步，进展；使（任务，事业）取得持续进展；**
    
    - **progress bar：进度条；**
    
    - **make progress ：取得进展；前进**
    
    - **go head、make headway：取得进展；前进**
    
    - **make progress in ：在……方面取得进步，取得进展**





## lesson 51

1. The strong wind<u><font color=red><strong>      has been blowing       </strong></font></u>on the lake and it doesn't seem to stop today, so they decide to put off the dragon-boat race. (blow)

   湖上**一直吹着大风，**看起来今天好像不会停了,所以他们决定推迟龙舟比赛。

   <font color=red><strong>has been blowing</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由题意可知,blow 是从过去一直持续进行到现在而且还有可能继续下去的动作，故用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

   1. **Put on: 穿上，戴上**

      - **She put on her coat before going outside.**
      - **He put on his glasses to read the small print.**

   2. **Put off: 推迟，延迟**

      - **They had to put off the meeting until next week.**
      - **Don't put off doing your homework until the last minute.**

   3. **Put away: 收起，放好**

      - **Please put away your toys when you're finished playing.**
      - **He put the books away on the shelf.**

   4. **Put up: 搭建，张贴**

      - **They put up a tent in the camping area.**
      - **The company put up posters to advertise the event.**

   5. **Put down: 放下，写下**

      - **She put down her bag and sat on the sofa.**
      - **He put his thoughts down on paper.**

   6. **Put forward: 提出，提议**

      - **He put forward a suggestion during the meeting.**
      - **They put forward their ideas for the project.**

   7. **Put in: 安装，投入**

      - **We need to put in a new air conditioning system.**
      - **He put in a lot of effort to make the project successful.**

   8. **Put off by: 对...感到厌烦或不悦**

      - **I was put off by his rude behavior.**

      - **The bad weather put us off from going outside.**

        

   **表示推迟的常见表达包括：**

   1. **Postpone: 推迟，延期**
      - **The meeting has been postponed until next week.**
      - **Due to bad weather, the flight has been postponed.**
   2. **Delay: 延迟，耽搁**
      - **The train is delayed by 30 minutes.**
      - **We apologize for the delay in the delivery of your package.**
   3. **Reschedule: 重新安排时间，改期**
      - **Let's reschedule the appointment for a later date.**
      - **The concert has been rescheduled to next month.**
   4. **Put off: 推迟，延期**
      - **They had to put off the event due to unforeseen circumstances.**
      - **Don't put off your tasks; complete them on time.**
   5. **Defer: 推迟，延期**
      - **The decision has been deferred until the next board meeting.**
      - **The project start date has been deferred by two weeks.**

2. -----What does the notice on the wall say?

   ----“No person<u><font color=red><strong>       shall take books out         </strong></font></u>of the reading room; otherwise he would be fined." (take)

   -----  墙上的通知说的什么?

   ------ 任何人不**得将图书带出**阅览室，否则将受到惩罚。

   <font color=red><strong>shall take books out</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>shall 用于第三人称作主语的陈述句中,表示要求、规定、法律等中的义务。</strong></font>

   1. **notice** 

      **n.注意，察觉；通告，布告；公告牌，警示牌；**

      **v.意识，注意；留意；正式通知**

      **without notice 不预先通知地；没有事先通知**

   2. **notify to ：向……报告**

      **Well, I will notify to the foreman.** 

      **好的，我会通知指导员的。**

   3. **fine**

      **adj.令人满意的，可以接受的；**

      **adv.很好；精致地，精美地；细小地**

      **v.罚款，处以罚金；使变纯**
      
      

   **"Shall" 是一个情态动词，用于表达将来时态、建议、命令、义务等含义。下面是 "shall" 的一些常见用法：**

   1. **将来时态：在正式的英语中，"shall" 可以用于表示将来时态，特别是在第一人称（我/我们）中。例如：**
      - **I shall arrive tomorrow.（我明天将到达。）**
      - **We shall discuss this matter further.（我们将进一步讨论这个问题。）**
   2. **建议："shall" 可以用于表示提出建议或提议。通常用于第一人称（我/我们）。例如：**
      - **Shall we go to the movies tonight?（今晚我们去看电影好吗？）**
      - **Shall I help you with your homework?（我帮你做作业吧？）**
   3. **命令和规定：在正式文件、法律文件或合同中，"shall" 可以用于表示命令、规定或义务。例如：**
      - **All employees shall wear a uniform.（所有员工都应该穿制服。）**
      - **The tenant shall pay the rent on the first day of each month.（租户应在每月的第一天支付租金。）**

   **需要注意的是，随着时间的推移，"shall" 在口语中的使用逐渐减少，大部分情况下被 "will" 所取代。因此，在口语中，往往使用 "will" 来表示将来时态和提出建议。**

3. I will go to Beijing on business tomorrow. Do you have anything <u><font color=red><strong>      to be taken          </strong></font></u> to your son in Beijing University? (take)

   我明天将去北京出差。你有什么东西**要带给**在北京大学的儿子吗?

   <font color=red><strong>to be taken</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>anything 与 take 是被动关系，且 take 是发生在将来的动作,故用不定式的被动式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

4. Contrary to popular belief, taking a walk immediately after meals doesn't necessarily <u><font color=red><strong>    do good to     </strong></font></u> our health. (do)

   与普遍的看法相反，饭后立刻散步不一定**对**我们的健康**有益**。

   <font color=red><strong>do good to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>do good to“对......有益处”。</strong></font>

   1. **Contrary** 

      - ***adj.*相反的，相对的；乖戾的，好与人作对的；逆向的，逆行的**
      - ***n.*相反的事实（或事情、情况）；对立命题，反对命题**
      - ***adv.*相反地**

   2. **contrary to**

      **与……相反，违反**

   3. **popular**

      ***adj.*受大众喜爱的，受欢迎的；（想法、情绪或态度）普遍的；通俗的，**

      **be popular with ：为……所喜欢；受……欢迎**

   4. **popularity**

      ***n.*流行，普及，受欢迎**
      **Today's lecture is about the popularity of English.** 

      **今天的讲座是关于英语的普及**

   5. **majority of**

      **The majority of the time, I brown-bagged my lunch.** 

      **大多数时间，我都是自带午餐。**

   6. **necessarily**

      **adv. 必定，必然；必要地**

   7. **belief**

      **n. 相信，信心；看法，信念，观点；信仰，信条**

5. -----Excuse me, sir, could you show me the ballpoint pen on the shelf?

   ----Well,<u><font color=red><strong>      writing smoothly      </strong></font></u>，it is very popular with the students. (smoothly)

   ------你好,先生，你能把架子上的那只圆珠笔拿给我看看吗?

   ------这笔**写起来流畅**，它很受学生的欢迎。

   <font color=red><strong>writing smoothly</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it 和 write 是逻辑上的主动关系，故用动词-ing 形式作状语。</strong></font>

6. Believe it or not, my missing wallet was found<u><font color=red><strong>   where we parted      </strong></font></u>last night. (part)

   信不信由你，我的钱包在**我们**昨晚**分开的地方**找到了。

   <font color=red><strong>where we parted</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>found 后缺少地点状语,故用 where 引导地点状语从句。</strong></font>

   1. **Separate: 分开，分离**

      - **They decided to separate and live in different cities.**
      - **The curtains separate the living room from the dining area.**

   2. **Split: 分开，分离**

      - **The group split into two smaller teams.**
      - **After the argument, they decided to split up and go their separate ways.**

   3. **Break up: 分手，分开**

      - **They recently broke up after being in a relationship for three years.**
      - **The band decided to break up and pursue individual careers.**

   4. **Part: 分道扬镳，分手**

      - **After traveling together for a while, they decided to part ways.**
      - **We parted at the airport**

   5. **Divorce: 离婚**

      - **They went through a difficult divorce and are now legally separated.**
      - **After years of unhappiness, they finally decided to divorce.**

   6. **part :** 

      **n.部分；某物的部分（局部）**

      **v.（使）分开，（使）分离；分别；分手；放弃，移交；给（头发）分缝**

      **adv.既有……又有……（part sth., part sth.）；不完全地，部分地**

      **adj.部分的，不完全的**

7. She doesn't look like<u><font color=red><strong>       what she was      </strong></font></u>a few years ago. As we can see, she can hardly be recognized. (be)

   她不像几年前的**样子**了。我们可以看出她很难被认出来。

   <font color=red><strong>what she was</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>look like 后为表语从句，引导词在从句中作表语，且指“样貌”,故用 what 引导。</strong></font>

8. I believe he is a great writer. I am now eagerly waiting his new novel to<u><font color=red><strong>     come out         </strong></font></u>.(come)

   我相信他是一个伟大的作家。我现在正急切地等待他的新小说**出版**。

   <font color=red><strong>come out</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>come out“出版，发行”无被动语态。</strong></font>

   **eagerly ：*adv.*急切地；渴望地；热心地**

   1. **publish ：出版，发行（书、杂志等）；（作家、 音乐家等）发表（自己的作品）**

      **They publish reference books.** 

      **他们出版参考书。**

   2. **appear ：*v.*出现，呈现；首次使用，起源；出庭；**

      **She will appear in court tomorrow.** 

      **她明天出庭。**

   3. **come out ：“出版，发行”无被动语态**

      **When does her new book come out?** 

      **她的新书什么时候出版？**

   4. **come off the press**

      **It will come off the press in the first half of next year.** 

      **它明年上半年可以出版。**

9. The farm as well as its neighboring hills<u><font color=red><strong>     has taken      </strong></font></u>on a new look recently. (take)

   近来这个农场和它附近的群山**呈现出**了一番新的面貌。

   <font color=red><strong>has taken</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>当主语带有 as well as...短语时,谓语动词不受其影响仍然和主语保持一致，故此处用单数;由 recently 可知,take 是到现在为止的动作，故用现在完成时。</strong></font>

   **neighboring ：**

   - **adj. 邻近的；附近的（等于 neighbouring）**
   - **v. 与……为邻；位于附近（neighbor 的 ing 形式）**

   **take on ：承担；呈现；具有；流行；接纳；雇用；穿上**

   **I can't take on any extra work.** 

   **我不能承担任何额外工作。**

10. <u><font color=red><strong>       In terms of      </strong></font></u>property, we are among the richest people in this city.  (terms)

    **在**财产**方面**,我们是这个城市最富有的人。
    
    <font color=red><strong>In terms of</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>in terms of“在.....·方面”。</strong></font>
    
    **property : *n.*所有物，财产；地产，房地产；房地产股票（或投资）**
    
    **properties：<法律> 所有权，处置权；特性，性质**
    
    **among ：prep. 在……当中，周围是；与……在一起；……之一；在……群体中；为……所共有；彼此间；以及**





##  lesson 52

1. 一Could you say anything about why you didn't pass the exam?

   一I have nothing to say. I<u><font color=red><strong>      did work        </strong></font></u>hard. ( work)

   一你能说说为什么考试没及格吗?

   一没什么可说的。我**的确**努力**工作**过。

   <font color=red><strong>did work</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由句意可知,work是过去发生的动作，故用一般过去时,强调谓语用助动词did。</strong></font>

2. “In no condition <u><font color=red><strong>     should you forget     </strong></font></u> you are an American.”Father told me before I went abroad“. (forget)

   在我出国前爸爸对我说:“在任何情况下**你**都不能**忘记**你是一一个美国人。”

   <font color=red><strong>should you forget</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示否定意义的介短语 in no condition置于句首时,句子用部分倒装。</strong></font>

   1. **In no way: 绝对不**
   2. **Under no circumstances: 在任何情况下都不**
   3. **On no account: 决不**
   4. **By no means: 绝不**
   5. **At no time: 任何时候都不**
   6. **In no uncertain terms: 毫不含糊地**
   7. **In no way, shape, or form: 绝对不，无论如何都不**
   8. **In no event: 在任何情况下都不**

   这些短语通常用于强调否定或排除可能性，表示某种情况绝对不会发生或不被接受。它们可以用于否定陈述、警告、拒绝或强调对某个行为或事件的限制。

3. It was so foggy that the driver could hardly <u><font color=red><strong>     make out       </strong></font></u> the way ahead. (make)

   雾特别大以至于司机几乎**辨认**不**出**前方的路。

   <font color=red><strong>make out</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>make out“辨认出,看出”。</strong></font>

   **foggy ：*adj.*有雾的，雾气茫茫的；迷糊的，朦胧的；模糊的，糊涂的**

   **fog ： *n.*雾；烟雾，尘雾；困惑，迷惘；（底片等的）灰雾，雾翳；*v.*使令人困惑，使费解；底片产生灰雾；**

4. Outside the school gate stood lots of parents,<u><font color=red><strong>      waiting for     </strong></font></u>their children. (wait)

   学校门口外站着很多**等待**孩子的父母。

   <font color=red><strong>waiting for/who were waiting for</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>主句介词在句首，句子完全倒装；句子主语 parents 与 wait是逻辑上的主动关系，故用动词-ing形式作定语，表示主动进行意义;</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>也可以看成是非限制性定语从句,引导词在从句中作主语，指代 parents，表示正在进行，故用 who were waiting for.</strong></font>

5. It has been announced that passengers<u><font color=red><strong>    mustn't open        </strong></font></u>their seatbelts until the plane has landed.(open)

   已经宣布,在飞机着陆之前乘客**禁止解开**安全带

   <font color=red><strong>mustn't open</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>mustn't“不许,禁止”。</strong></font>

   **"must" 可以使用否定形式。否定形式为 "must not" 或缩写形式 "mustn't"。它表示禁止、不允许或强烈不建议做某事。"mustn't" 是 "must not" 的缩写形式，用于口语和非正式场合。在正式写作或正式场合中，更常用完整形式 "must not"。**

   **announced ：**

   - **adj. 宣布的**
   - **v. 宣布，宣告；通知；声称，宣称；宣布（某人）到达；（在广播或电视中）播音，广播（announce 的过去式和过去分词）**

6. ---When can I use your computer?

   ---Never!<u><font color=red><strong>     At no time        </strong></font></u>should you touch it. (time)

   ----我什么时候能用-下你的电脑?

   ----不行!你**绝不**能碰它。

   <font color=red><strong>At no time</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>at no time“绝不,从不”。</strong></font>

7. ---Jim will be present at our party tonight.

   ---Don't be so sure. He<u><font color=red><strong>      might/may stay at       </strong></font></u>home looking after his sick mother. (stay)

   ---吉姆今晚会来参加我们的聚会。

   ---不要这么确定。他**可能待在**家照顾他生病的妈妈。

   <font color=red><strong>might/may stay at</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>此处表示对将来情况把握性不大的推测,用 might 或 may。</strong></font>

   表达 "出席、出现、参加" 的常见短语和词组包括：

   1. **Attend：出席**
   2. **Be present：出席、在场**
   3. **Show up：出现、露面**
   4. **Turn up：出现、到场**
   5. **Participate in：参与、参加**
   6. **Take part in：参与、参加**
   7. **Join：加入、参加**
   8. **Be in attendance：出席**
   9. **Be in the presence of：在某人的面前**
   10. **Be at the event：在活动现场**
   11. **Be a part of：是其中的一员**
   12. **Be involved in：参与其中**
   13. **Be engaged in：从事、参与**
   14. **Be present at：在...出席**

8. Have you gone beyond the stage<u><font color=red><strong>     when you want to     </strong></font></u>stop smoking but you can't? (want)

   你是不是过了戒烟**欲罢**不能的**阶段**了?

   <font color=red><strong>when you want to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>定语从的先行词是表示时间的名词stage,引导词在从句中作时间状语,故用 when;want to do sth.“想做某事”</strong></font>

   **beyond ：prep. 在（或向）……较远的一边；晚于，迟于；adv. 在另一边，在（或向）更远处；（延续）到……之后**

9. If you have to catch the first bus every day, choose this hotel.<u><font color=red><strong>        It is very convenient        </strong></font></u>for the station ------- it's only two minutes' walk.(convenient)

   如果你想每天乘坐第一辆公交车,请选择这个宾馆。这儿到车站**很方便,**仅有两分钟的路程。

   <font color=red><strong>It is very convenient</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>It is convenient for. ...“.....·近便的；It is convenient for me to have a supermarket right next to my house.（我家旁边有一家超市对我来说很方便。）”.</strong></font>

   **convenience ：*n.*方便，便利；便利的事物，便利设施；公共厕所**

   **convenient ：*adj.*方便的，便利的；附近的，方便到达的；**

10. 一How about going camping tomorrow?

    一I suppose not, because I <u><font color=red><strong>     am suffering from      </strong></font></u> a bad cold. (suffer)

    一明天去野营怎么样?

    一恐怕不行，因为我**正蒙受着**感冒。
    
    <font color=red><strong>am suffering from</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>由句意可知，“感冒”是目前正发生的动作,故用现在进行时。</strong></font>
    
    **suppose ：v. 推断，料想，猜想；假设，假定，设想；预期，需要，以……为条件；相信，认为（某事物是可能的）；（婉转表达）我看，要我说，要不；（因处于某种境地或因约定）必须做（be supposed to do sth.）；我看（用于生气地表示预料某事属实）**





##  lesson 53

1. The idea they have come up with sounds great, but it remains <u><font color=red><strong>     to be seen       </strong></font></u>whether it works well in practice. (see)

   他们提出的观点听起来很好，但是**还有待看看**它是否在实际中运行良好。

   <font color=red><strong>to be seen</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>it指代the idea,与see是逻辑上的被动关系,目see是表示将要发生的动作,故用不定式的被动式作表语。</strong></font>

   1. **remain ：v. 逗留，留下；剩余，遗留；保持不变，一直是；仍需去做（或处理）n. 剩余（物），遗迹；遗体，残骸**

   2. **remind ：v. 提醒，使想起；（因相像）使联想起（remind sb. of）**

   3. **in practice ：在实践中；实际上，事实上**

   4. **"Come up with" 和 "put forward"**

      1. **Come up with:**
         - **含义：提出，想出，找到**
         - **用法：指通过思考、创造或努力产生某个想法、策略、解决方案等。**
         - **例句：**
           - **He always comes up with creative ideas for our projects. （他总是能为我们的项目想出创意的主意。）**
           - **Can you come up with a name for our new product? （你能给我们的新产品想一个名字吗？）**
      2. **Put forward:**
         - **含义：提出，提议**
         - **用法：指正式地提出或提议某个想法、观点、计划等，通常用于讨论、辩论、会议等正式场合。**
         - **例句：**
           - **She put forward a suggestion to improve the company's efficiency. （她提出了一个提高公司效率的建议。）**
           - **The committee will put forward their recommendations at the meeting. （委员会将在会议上提出他们的建议。）**

      **这两个词组都强调提出某个观点或主意，但 "come up with" 更加强调从个人的思考、创造中得出想法，而 "put forward" 则更多用于正式的场合和团体讨论中提出建议或观点。**

   5. **表达方式来表示提出想法、建议或观点的词组。**

      1. **Propose: 提议，建议**
         - **She proposed a new marketing strategy for the company. （她为公司提出了一项新的营销策略。）**
      2. **Suggest: 建议，暗示**
         - **He suggested having a team meeting to discuss the issue. （他建议开一个团队会议来讨论这个问题。）**
      3. **Present: 提出，呈现**
         - **The research team presented their findings at the conference. （研究团队在会议上呈现了他们的研究结果。）**
      4. **Advance: 提出，提倡**
         - **He advanced a theory that challenged the current understanding of the phenomenon. （他提出了一个挑战当前对该现象的理解的理论。）**
      5. **Offer: 提出，提供**
         - **She offered a solution to the problem that nobody had considered before. （她提出了一个以前没有人考虑过的问题解决方案。）**

   

2. I suffered in the earthquake last week and only then<u><font color=red><strong>        did I realize        </strong></font></u>the value of life. (realize)

   上周我遭遇了一场地震，只有那时我**才意识到**生命的价值。

   <font color=red><strong>did I realize</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>only修饰的时间状语置于首时句子要用部分倒装;此处表示过去发生的动作,应用一般过去时；only then ：直到那时……（后面的句子要倒装）</strong></font>

   **"suffer from" 和 "suffer in" 是两个不同的短语，用来描述经历疼痛、困难或负面情况。**

   1. **"suffer from"：这个短语用来表示某人正在经历特定的疾病、状况或问题。通常与与健康相关的问题一起使用。**

      **He suffers from migraines.（他患有偏头痛。）**

   2. **"suffer in"：这个短语用来描述在特定情况或环境中处于困扰或困难中的状态。它暗示在该情境下经历困难或不适。**

      **The workers suffered in harsh working conditions. （工人们在恶劣的工作条件下受苦。）**

   **总结起来，"suffer from" 用来指示经历特定的疾病或情况，而"suffer in" 用来描述在特定情况下忍受困难或困苦。**

3. They are determined to rebuild<u><font color=red><strong>     what was destroyed       </strong></font></u>in the earthquake. (destroy)

   他们决定重建在地震中**被毁坏的一切**。

   <font color=red><strong>what was destroyed/all that was destroyed</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>rebuild后的宾语从句中缺少主语,故用what引导;也可看成是定语从句先行词是all,引导词用that引导；从句是宾语从句，不是定语从句，所以不能用非谓语动词省略</strong></font>

   **"be determined to do" 和 "Determine to do" 都表示决心要做某事，但在用法上有一些区别。**

   1. **"be determined to do" 是一个形容词短语，用来描述一个人已经下定决心要做某事。其中的 "be" 是系动词，用来连接 "determined"（表示决心）和 "to do"（表示要做的事情）。**

      **例如：他决心要学好英语。- He is determined to learn English.**

   2. **"Determine to do" 是一个动词短语，其中的 "determine" 是一个动词，意思是 "决定" 或 "确定"，后面跟着 "to do" 表示要做的事情。这个短语表示做出决定或下定决心要做某事。例如：他决定要去旅行。- He determined to go on a trip.**

   **总结：**

   - **"be determined to do" 表示一个人已经下定决心要做某事，强调状态或属性。**
   - **"Determine to do" 表示做出决定或下定决心要做某事，强调动作或行为。**

4. The government is taking measures<u><font color=red><strong>     to improve     </strong></font></u>the air quality of our city. (improve)

   政府正采取措施**改善**我们城市的空气质量。

   <font color=red><strong>to improve</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>“采取措施”的目的是“改善我们城市的空气质量”,且government与improve是逻辑上的主动关系，故用不定式的一般式作目的状语。</strong></font>

   **"measure" 是一个多义词，具有多种用法。以下是几个常见的用法：**

   1. **作为名词：**
      - **"measure" 可表示 "措施"、"方法"、"步骤"，用于描述为达到某个目的所采取的行动或方式。例如：We need to take measures to protect the environment.（我们需要采取措施来保护环境。）**
      - **"measure" 还可以指 "尺寸" 或 "度量单位"，用于测量长度、面积、体积等。例如：The length of the room is 10 meters as per the measuring tape.（根据测量带，房间的长度是10米。）**
   2. **作为动词：**
      - **"measure" 作为动词可以表示 "测量"、"衡量"、"评估"。例如：They measured the distance between the two points.（他们测量了两点之间的距离。）**
      - **"measure" 还可以表示 "采取措施"、"评估风险"。例如：We must measure the potential risks before making a decision.（在做出决定之前，我们必须评估潜在的风险。）**
   3. **其他常见表达：**
      - **"take measures" 指采取行动或措施以解决问题或应对情况。例如：The government has taken measures to improve public safety.（政府已经采取了措施来提高公共安全。）**
      - **"beyond measure" 表示超过计量范围，意为 "无法估量" 或 "极其大量"。例如：Her love for him was beyond measure.（她对他的爱是无法估量的。）**

5. You<u><font color=red><strong>       could have caught         </strong></font></u>the last bus, but you were clearly in no hurry. (catch)

   你**本来能够赶上**最后一班公共汽车的,但是你明显一点儿也不着急。

   <font color=red><strong>could have caught</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示过去本能够做某事但实际上没做用 could have done.</strong></font>

   **clearly ：adv. 清楚地，清晰地；毫无疑问，显然；明智地，清醒地**

   **clear ：*adj.*易懂的，明白的；完全了解的，清楚的；（物质）透明的，清澈的**

   **in no hurry：不着急；不匆忙**

   **Take it easy**
   **从容；不急；松懈；**

   **Take your time**
   **别着急；从容做；**

   **no hurry**
   **不忙；不必着急；**

6. I keep on walking after supper because I can't think of<u><font color=red><strong>       a better way      </strong></font></u>to keep fit. (good)

   晚饭后我总是去散步，因为我想不出**一个更好的**保持健康的好方法。

   <font color=red><strong>a better way</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>形容词的比较级用于否定中表示最高级意义。</strong></font>

   **keep on doing ：继续做某事；继续做**

   **think of ：记起，想起；考虑；想像；关心**

7. Mary can't invite you to her new house until she<u><font color=red><strong>       has moved         </strong></font></u>in.(move)

   直到玛丽**搬进**新家之后她才会邀请你去她家。

   <font color=red><strong>has moved</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>move 是在将来某个时间点之前要完成的动作在时间状语从句中,常用现在完成时表示将来完成意义。</strong></font>

   **一般来说，主句和从句的时态可以根据具体语境和需要进行调整。下面是一些常见的时态搭配：**

   1. **主句使用一般现在时，从句使用一般现在时：**
      - **I won't leave the office until I finish this report.（直到我完成这份报告，我才会离开办公室。）**
   2. **主句使用一般过去时，从句使用过去完成时或者一般过去式：**
      - **She didn't realize her mistake until she had already submitted the report.（直到她已经提交了报告，她才意识到自己的错误。）**
      - **They didn't meet each other until they both joined the same club.（直到他们都加入了同一个俱乐部，他们才相遇。）**
   3. **主句使用一般将来时，从句使用将来完成时：**
      - **We won't start the meeting until everyone has arrived.（直到每个人都到齐，我们才开始会议。）**

8. She must have ranked her birthday presents <u><font color=red><strong>       in order of           </strong></font></u> preference because the top one is her favorite. (order)

   她一定把生日礼物**按照**喜欢程度的**顺序**排列好了，因为最顶端的是她最喜欢的。

   <font color=red><strong>in order of</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>in order of“按....·的顺序”。</strong></font>

   **preference ：n. 偏爱，偏好；更喜欢的人（或物）；优待，优先（权）；<法律>（尤指债务偿付）优先偿还权**

9. My toothache<u><font color=red><strong>         is killing me      </strong></font></u>.I thought it was going away, but it is getting worse now.(kill)

   我的牙齿**疼得我要命**。我以为它已经好了,但没想到现在越来越糟糕了。

   <font color=red><strong>is killing me</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>kill是现在正在进行的动作，故用现在进行时。</strong></font>

10. Keep in mind that you should do the same things<u><font color=red><strong>    as are listed        </strong></font></u>in the instructions. (list)

    要记住你应该**按照**说明上**列的**去做同样的事情。

    <font color=red><strong>as are listed</strong></font>

    <strong>解析：</strong>

    <font color=red><strong>定语从句的先行词是things,引导词在从句中作主语，先行词things前有the same修饰，故只能用as;things与list之间是被动关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>
    
    **Keep in mind that ：记住……，牢记……**
    
    **the same...as..." 是一个常用的句型，用来比较两个或多个事物之间的相似性。它的基本结构是 "the same + noun + as + noun"，其中第一个名词是用来修饰第二个名词的，表示它们具有相同的特征或属性。**
    
    **下面是一些例子，展示了 "the same...as..." 的用法：**
    
    1. **形容词的比较：**
       - **She has the same hairstyle as her sister.（她和她姐姐有相同的发型。）**
       - **This book is not the same size as the previous one.（这本书和前一本的尺寸不一样。）**
    2. **名词的比较：**
       - **He is wearing the same shirt as me.（他穿着和我一样的衬衫。）**
       - **Our cars are the same make as yours.（我们的车和你们的是同款的。）**
    3. **动词的比较：**
       - **They have the same interests as us.（他们和我们有相同的兴趣。）**
       - **Sarah can swim as well as her brother.（Sarah和她的哥哥一样会游泳。）**
    
    **需要注意的是，在比较中，"the same...as..." 结构中的两个名词通常是同类事物，用于表达它们之间的相似性。**





##  lesson 54

1. He came all the way on such a rainy night, mainly <u><font color=red><strong>     to make sure         </strong></font></u> that everything was going on right. (make)

   在这样的一个雨天他走完了全程，主要是**为了确保**切都运行正常。

   <font color=red><strong>to make sure</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>此处表示目的，且表示将要发生的动作，故用不定式的一般式作目的状语。</strong></font>

   1. **Rain：指雨水，表示降水的现象。例如："It's raining outside."（外面正在下雨。）**
   2. **Rainy：形容词，意为多雨的，表示天气有雨的。例如："It's a rainy day."（这是一个多雨的日子。）**
   3. **Snow：指雪，表示降雪的现象。例如："It's snowing heavily."（正在下大雪。）**
   4. **Snowy：形容词，意为有雪的，表示地面被雪覆盖的情况。例如："We went for a walk in the snowy forest."（我们在雪覆盖的森林里散步。）**
   5. **Cloud：指云，表示天空中的气象现象。例如："The sky is full of clouds."（天空布满了云。）**
   6. **Cloudy：形容词，意为多云的，表示天气多云的状态。例如："It's a cloudy day, but it's not raining."（这是一个多云的日子，但没有下雨。）**

   **这些词汇描述了不同的天气和天气现象。"Rain"和"snow"是名词，表示具体的降水或降雪现象，而"rainy"和"snowy"是形容词，用于描述天气的状态。"Cloud"指的是天空中的云，而"cloudy"表示天气多云的状态。**

2. Though frightened at the sight of the hungry lion, Mary managed to hold onto herself and didn't scream. The lion, otherwise,  <u><font color=red><strong>       would have attacked       </strong></font></u> her. (attack)

   尽管看见饥饿的狮子玛丽很害怕，但是她成功地稳住了? 自己而且没有大声尖叫。否则狮子**就会袭击**她了。

   <font color=red><strong>would have attacked</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>从句以"Though"开头，表示虽然。因为主句从句主语相同，所以省略从句主语使用非谓语动词，"frightened"是过去分词作为表语，表示感到害怕。由otherwise可知，此处为含蓄虚拟语气，表示与过去事实相反的假设，故谓语动词用would have done的形式。</strong></font>

   1. **at the sight of ：一看见……就**

      **His heart lifted at the sight of her.** 

      **他一看见她心里就高兴起来了。**

   2. **hold onto ：紧紧抓住，抓住不放；保持住**

      **I'll hold onto your mail for you until you get back**

3. The shop owner promised me that he<u><font color=red><strong>        would inform      </strong></font></u>me as soon as the product became available.(inform)

   店主向我许诺一旦有了产品就**将**立刻**通知**我。

   <font color=red><strong>would inform</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由意可知,inform 表示的动作是从过去看将要发生的,故用过去将来时。</strong></font>

   **as soon as ：一……就……**

   **I'll call you as soon as I know. 我一知道就给你打电话。**

4. It was this wonderful place<u><font color=red><strong>     where I spent       </strong></font></u>my childhood that I got to know my lifelong friend Lucy. (spend)

   正是在**我度过**童年的美丽**的地方**我认识了一生的朋友露西。

   <font color=red><strong>where/in which I spent</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>定语从句的先行词是表示地点的名词 place,引导词在从句中作地点状语,故用where,相当于in which.</strong></font>

5. The mountain scenery<u><font color=red><strong>        is typical of          </strong></font></u>Scotland, which is bound to attract tourists from other parts of the world. (typical)

   这是**典型**的苏格兰山区景色,注定要吸引来自世界各地的游客。

   <font color=red><strong>is typical of</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>typical“典型的,有代表性的”,后面常跟介词of搭配。</strong></font>

   - **scenery ：n. 风景，景色；舞台布景**

   - **is typical of ：是…的特点；典型的**

     **This meal is typical of local cookery.** 

     **这是有当地风味的饭菜。**

   - **be bound to ：必然；一定要**

     **This package needs to be bound to a collection ID.** 

     **这个包需要绑定到一个集合id。**

   - **Other parts of ：用来指代除了提到的部分之外的其他部分或方面。**

6. With odd behavior and strange ideas, Henry can't <u><font color=red><strong>       be made out        </strong></font></u>by most of his fellow workers.(make)

   由于怪诞的行为和奇怪的想法，亨利不**被**他的大部分同事**所理解。**

   <font color=red><strong>be made out</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>with引导一个介词短语作为状语修饰整个句子；make out“理解”,Henry 与 make out 之间是被动关系,用被动语态。</strong></font>

   **fellow ：n. 小伙子，家伙；同伴，同事，同学；研究员；男朋友；adj. 同类的，同伴的**

   1. **All of: 所有的**
      - **All of the students passed the exam. (所有的学生都通过了考试。)**
   2. **None of: 没有任何**
      - **None of the books on the shelf are mine. (书架上没有任何一本是我的。)**
   3. **Any of: 任何一个**
      - **You can choose any of the available options. (你可以选择任何一个可用的选项。)**
   4. **Both of: 两者都**
      - **Both of my parents attended the meeting. (我的父母双方都参加了会议。)**
   5. **Either of: 两者中的任何一个**
      - **You can take either of the two routes to reach the destination. (你可以选择两条路线中的任何一条来到达目的地。)**
   6. **Neither of: 两者都不**
      - **Neither of the options is suitable for me. (这两个选项都不适合我。)**
   7. **One of: 其中之一**
      - **She is one of my closest friends. (她是我最亲密的朋友之一。)**
   8. **Most of: 大部分**
      - **Most of the guests arrived late to the party. (大部分客人都迟到了。)**
   9. **Some of: 一些**
      - **Some of the students participated in the school event. (一些学生参加了学校活动。)**

7. It is required that under no circumstances<u><font color=red><strong>         should we betray        </strong></font></u>our country even if there are temptations like money or beauty. (betray)

   要求在任何情况下**我们**也不**应该背叛**我们的国家，即使有金钱或美色的诱惑。

   <font color=red><strong>should we betray</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>表示否定意义的介词短语under no circumstances置于句首时，句子用部分倒装;It is required that...句式中要用虚拟语气，谓语动词用“should+动词原形”,should可以省略,故此处的助动词用should。</strong></font>

   1. **Under no circumstances 用于强调某种绝对的否定或限制条件。它表示在任何情况下都不会发生或被允许。这个短语常用于警告、规定或强调某种禁止或限制。在句首时后面句子要部分倒装**
   2. **temptation ：n. 引诱，诱惑；诱惑人的东西；（魔鬼对耶稣的）引诱（the Temptation）**

8. Yesterday we visited a modern school,<u><font color=red><strong>       around which are    </strong></font></u>some bookstores. (around)

   昨天我们参观了一所现代中学,**它周围**有一些书店。

   <font color=red><strong>around which are</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>根据提示词及句意可知，此是“around+关系代词”引导的非限制性定语从句,先行词是 school,引导词用 which;定语从句的主语是some bookstores,故谓语动词用复数形式。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>从句的主要原因是介词短语"around which"位于句首，这导致了部分倒装。原本的词序应该是"some bookstores are around which"。</strong></font>

9. We are all surprised to see him drive a Benz. Who knows<u><font color=red><strong>      how he got         </strong></font></u>so much money to afford it? (get)

   我们都惊讶的发现他开着奔驰车，谁知道**他如何得到**这么多钱买的车。

   <font color=red><strong>how he got</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>knows 后的宾语从句中缺少方式状语,故引导词用how,宾语从句中用陈述语序。</strong></font>

   **be surprised to do sth：对做某事感到惊奇吃惊地做某事惊讶地做某事**

10. On the playground, each competitor<u><font color=red><strong>      shall wear        </strong></font></u>a number to be recognized. (wear)

    在操场上，每一位参赛者都**要戴**一个号码牌以便识别。
    
    <font color=red><strong>shall wear</strong></font>
    
    <strong>解析：</strong>
    
    <font color=red><strong>shall 用于主语为第三人称的陈述句中,表示命令、要求、规定等中的义务；to be recognized表目的</strong></font>
    
    **competitor ：n. 竞争者，对手；选手，参赛者**
    
    **在操场上，你要戴一个号码牌以便识别 ：On the playground, you need to wear a number plate for identification**





## lesson 55

1. The Amazon valley is very important to the natural balance of the earth. Forty percent of the world's oxygen <u><font color=red><strong>       is produced        </strong></font></u> there, (produce)

   亚马逊山谷对地球的自然生态平衡是非常重要的。地球上40%的氧气**产生**在那里。

   <font color=red><strong>is produced</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>oxygen与produce是被动关系，且表示客观事实,故用一般现在时的被动语态。</strong></font>

2. Parents are beyond question <u><font color=red><strong>      the most influential          </strong></font></u>people to their children. (influential)

   父母毫无疑问是对孩子**影响最大**的人。

   <font color=red><strong>the most influential</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>influential“有影响力的”,其最高级形式要借助most构成。</strong></font>

   1. **beyond question ：*adv.*毫无疑问；无可争辩**

      **You're right beyond question.** 

      **无可争辩，你是对的**

   2. **影响的表达方式：**

      1. **Have an impact on：**
         - **The new regulations will have a significant impact on the economy. （新的规定将对经济产生重大影响。）**
      2. **Affect：**
         - **The changes in weather patterns are affecting agricultural production. （天气模式的变化正在影响农业生产。）**
      3. **Influence：**
         - **Her words of encouragement influenced me to pursue my dreams. （她的鼓励之词影响了我追求梦想。）**

3. <u><font color=red><strong>       Having volunteered         </strong></font></u>to paint the house, John found it embarrassed to have to stop halfway.(volunteer)

   约翰**已自告奋勇**粉刷房子,他发现半途而废会很窘迫。

   <font color=red><strong>Having volunteered</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>John与volunteer是逻辑上的主动关系,且volunteer表示的动作发生在主谓语动词found表示的动作之前,故用动词-ing形式的的完成式。</strong></font>

   1. **volunteer**

      1. **n.志愿者，义务工作者；自告奋勇者**

      2. **v.自愿做，义务做，无偿做；志愿服役**

         **volunteer to do sth ：自愿做某事**

         **I volunteered to help clean up the park after the event. （我自愿帮助清理活动结束后的公园。）**

      3. **adj.志愿（者）的**

   2. **voluntary**

      ***adj.*自愿的，自发的，主动的；（机构或组织）志愿的，义务性的；**

4. A website claims<u><font color=red><strong>      to have uncovered      </strong></font></u>the top secret recipe of the big food company. （uncover)

   一个网站宣称**已经解开**了这个大型食品公司的绝密配方。

   <font color=red><strong>to have uncovered</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>claim“声称”,后面跟不定式作宾语uncover表示的动作发生在主谓语动词 claims 表示的动作之前,故用不定式的完成式。</strong></font>

   **claim ：v. 声称，断言；索取，索要（钱）；要求（拥有）n. 声称，断言；索要，索赔；权利，所有权；要求得到的土地使用权；专利新特征申明**

   - **[claim for sth](javascript:;) 要求；因某事索赔**
   - **claim to do 声称要做;声称做某事**

5. Going out to the bar and drinking<u><font color=red><strong>        is a way to        </strong></font></u>relax, but not good for your health at all.(way)

   去酒吧喝酒是放松的**一种方式**,但是对你的健康一点也不好。

   <font color=red><strong>is a way to</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>going out to the bar and drinking 是指件事谓语动词用单数;此处描述一般的情况,故用一般现在时;a way to do“做·....·的一个方法”。</strong></font>

   **a way to do sth :做·....·的一个方法**

   **Learning a foreign language is a way to expand your horizons and connect with people from different cultures.**

   **学习一门外语是拓展视野和与不同文化的人建立联系的一种方式。**

6. Don't <u><font color=red><strong>      blame John for          </strong></font></u>breaking the vase; he is a child after all.(blame)

   不要**责怪约翰**打碎了花瓶，毕竟他还是个孩子。

   <font color=red><strong>blame John for</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>blame sb.for “为·....·责怪某人”</strong></font>

   1. **blame**
      1. **Blame + for + 名词/动名词：表示因某事责备某人。**
         - **They blamed him for causing the accident. 他们责怪他引发了事故。**
      2. **Blame + on + 名词/代词：表示将责任推卸给某人或某事。**
         - **Don't blame your failures on others. 不要将你的失败归咎于他人。**
      3. **Take/accept the blame：表示承担责任或接受责备。**
         - **She was willing to take the blame for the mistake. 她愿意为错误承担责任。**
   2. **after all :毕竟；终究**

7. By the time you<u><font color=red><strong>       arrive in London         </strong></font></u>.we will have stayed in Europe for two weeks. (arrive)

   等你**到达伦敦**的时候，我们就已经在欧洲待了两周了。

   <font color=red><strong>arrive in London</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由will have stayed及意可知，arrive是表示将来的动作,在时间状语从句中,常用一般现在时表示将来意义;arrive in后面常接大的地方。</strong></font>

8. I was not in Beijing last June, otherwise I<u><font color=red><strong>     would not have missed         </strong></font></u>my son's graduation ceremony. (miss)

   去年六月我没有在北京，否则我是**不会错过**我儿子的毕业典礼的。

   <font color=red><strong>would not have missed</strong></font>

   <strong>解析：</strong>

   <font color=red><strong>由otherwise及意可知，此处表示与过去事实相反的情况，故谓语动词用would have done的形式，由句意知用否定形式。</strong></font>

   1. **graduation ：*n.*毕业；毕业典礼；**

   2. **graduate ：*n.*大学毕业生，学士学位获得者；毕业生 *v.*获得学位（尤指学士），大学毕业；毕业（尤指中学）；*adj.*（课程、学业）研究生的**

      **graduate from ：*v.*从……毕业**

   3. **graduate student : *n.*研究生；毕业生**

   4. **Major**

      - adj.主要的；严重的；大的，年长的；主修的；
      - n.主修科目，专业；陆军少校，（美国）空军少校；
      - v.（在美国大学）主修，专攻

      **I major in English：我主修英语**

      **My major is Business English : 我的专业是商务英语**

   5. **gradually ：*adv.*逐渐地，逐步地**

   6. **gradual ：*adj.*逐渐的，渐进的；平缓的，不陡的** 

9. It was not until the baby girl was sound asleep<u><font color=red><strong>      that her parents had (the) time        </strong></font></u>to deal with their personal affairs.(have)

   直到这个女婴睡熟了，**她的父母才有时间**处理自己的事情。
